ActBusy Script File
// "act busy name"		This is the name that a mapmaker must specify in the hint node.
// 	"busy_anim"			"Activity Name".
// 	"entry_anim"		"Activity Name"
// 	"exit_anim"			"Activity Name"
// 	"busy_sequence"		"Sequence Name". If specified, this is used over the activity name. Specify it in the hint node.
// 	"entry_sequence"	"Sequence Name". If specified, this is used over the entry anim.
// 	"exit_sequence"		"Sequence Name". If specified, this is used over the exit anim.
// 	"min_time"			"Minimum time to spend in this busy anim"
// 	"max_time"			"Maximum time to spend in this busy anim"	0 = only stop when interrupted by external event
// 	"interrupts"		One of:
// 						"BA_INT_NONE"		break out only when time runs out. No external influence will break me out.
// 						"BA_INT_DANGER"		break out of this anim only if threatened
// 						"BA_INT_PLAYER"		break out of this anim if I can see the player, or I'm threatened
// 						"BA_INT_AMBUSH"		someone please define this - I have no idea what it does
// 						"BA_INT_COMBAT"		break out of this anim if combat occurs in my line of sight (bullet hits, grenades, etc), -OR- the max time is reached
"ActBusy.txt"

CQAnimationPicker
IControlSelectionChangedListener
IQCTabbedObject
CQAnimationSetControlModel
NotProcedural!!!
Playhead
Release
Stagger
Zero: Blend each control towards 0.0
Default: Blend each control towards that control's default/neutral value
One: Blend each control towards 1.0
Half: Blend each control towards 0.5
In: Blend each control towards that control's value at the start of the time selection
Playhead: Blend each control towards that control's current value
Paste: Blend each control towards the values previously copied into the clipboard
Out: Blend each control towards that control's value at the end of the time selection
Jitter: Blend each control towards a copy of the control's values that have had noise added to them
Drop: Blend each control towards that control's values prior to starting the floating modification layer
Stagger: Retime each control by a random amount, to offset them from each other
Smooth: Blend each control towards a smoothed copy of the control's values
Release: Retime each control by shifting any animation in the falloff away from the hold region
Hold: Retime each control by shifting any animation in the falloff towards the hold region
Ramp: Blend each control towards a linear falloff between the start and end of the time selection's hold region
Steady: Retime each control's animation towards having a constant velocity
Round: Blend each control towards a spline fitted through the four time selection times
Spline: Blend each control towards a spline fitted through the control's values at the bookmarked times

<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.0//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/REC-html40/strict.dtd">
<html><head><meta name="qrichtext" content="1" /><style type="text/css">
p, li { white-space: pre-wrap; }
</style></head><body style=" font-family:'MS Shell Dlg 2'; font-size:12pt; font-weight:72; font-style:normal;">
<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">Copy &amp; Paste timing and motion blocks from a KeyValues file into the text box below. Refer to the example data to the right for the general format of the data.</span></p>
<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">The currently selected animation range is used to define the start and end frames which are adjusted and referred to by the cycle times defined below. The selected range can be modified by changing &quot;Frame Start&quot; and &quot;Frame End&quot; below.</span></p>
<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">Supported keys are listed below.</span></p>
<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:10pt; font-weight:600;">PlaybackRate</span></p>
<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">Playback rate is a single value which will cause the selected animation to run at the specified speed. Values less than 1 will cause the animation to run slower, values greater than one will cause the animation to run faster. e.g. A value of 2 will cause the animation to run twice as fast.</span></p>
<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:10pt; font-weight:600;">SetPlaybackRate</span></p>
<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">SetPlaybackRate is a series of blocks that contain two values; </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600;">Cycle</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;"> &amp; </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600;">PlaybackRate</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">. The cycle values for each block must not be duplicated and must be specified in order. These blocks modify the playback rate for the specific portion of the animation controlled by cycle. Cycle values are in the range of [0, 1] where 0 is the first frame of the animation and 1 is the last frame of animation.</span></p>
<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:10pt; font-weight:600;">OverrideMotion</span></p>
<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">OverrideMotion is a series of blocks that contain three supported values; </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600;">StartCycle</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">, </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600;">EndCycle</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;"> &amp; </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600;">MotionScale</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">. </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600; color:#aa0000;">Movement</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;"> parameters are ignored. OverrideMotion with a MotionScale value will scale the selectedtranslation values by the MotionScale value in the range of animation specified.</span></p></body></html>
<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.0//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/REC-html40/strict.dtd">
<html><head><meta name="qrichtext" content="1" /><style type="text/css">
p, li { white-space: pre-wrap; }
</style></head><body style=" font-family:'MS Shell Dlg 2'; font-size:8pt; font-weight:400; font-style:normal;">
<p style=" margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;">&quot;<span style=" font-weight:600;">SetPlaybackRate</span>&quot;</p>
<p style=" margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;">{</p>
<p style=" margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;">	&quot;Cycle&quot;	&quot;0.0&quot;</p>
<p style=" margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;">	&quot;PlaybackRate&quot;	&quot;0.3&quot;</p>
<p style=" margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;">}</p>
<p style=" margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;">&quot;<span style=" font-weight:600;">SetPlaybackRate</span>&quot;</p>
<p style=" margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;">{</p>
<p style=" margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;">	&quot;Cycle&quot;	&quot;0.1&quot;</p>
<p style=" margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;">	&quot;PlaybackRate&quot;	&quot;1.0&quot;</p>
<p style=" margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;">}</p>
<p style=" margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;">&quot;<span style=" font-weight:600;">SetPlaybackRate</span>&quot;</p>
<p style=" margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;">{</p>
<p style=" margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;">	&quot;Cycle&quot;	&quot;0.80&quot;</p>
<p style=" margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;">	&quot;PlaybackRate&quot;	&quot;0.5&quot;</p>
<p style=" margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;">}</p>
<p style="-qt-paragraph-type:empty; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><br /></p>
<p style=" margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;">&quot;<span style=" font-weight:600;">PlaybackRate</span>&quot;	&quot;1.5&quot;</p>
<p style="-qt-paragraph-type:empty; margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><br /></p>
<p style=" margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;">&quot;<span style=" font-weight:600;">OverrideMotion</span>&quot;</p>
